          "arguments": "{\"problem_statement\": \"# 🎯 Add Two-Step Transcript Selection Flow\\n\\n## Problem\\n\\nCurrently, the app blindly attempts to extract transcripts without knowing what's available. This leads to errors like \\\"Transcripts are disabled\\\" even when auto-generated subtitles exist.\\n\\nUsers have no control over:\\n- Which language to use (if multiple available)\\n- Manual vs auto-generated subtitles\\n\\n## Solution\\n\\nImplement **two-step flow**:\\n\\n### **Step 1: List Available Transcripts**\\nUser enters URL → Backend returns list of available transcripts (without downloading)\\n\\n### **Step 2: Extract Selected Transcript**\\nUser selects language + type → Backend downloads chosen transcript\\n\\n---\\n\\n## 📦 Backend Implementation\\n\\n### **1. New Endpoint: GET /api/transcripts/list**\\n\\n**Request:**\\n```\\nGET /api/transcripts/list?url=https://youtube.com/watch?v=VIDEO_ID\\n```\\n\\n**Response:**\\n```json\\n{\\n  \\\"video_id\\\": \\\"L-BgxLtMxh0\\\",\\n  \\\"video_url\\\": \\\"https://youtube.com/watch?v=L-BgxLtMxh0\\\",\\n  \\\"available_transcripts\\\": [\\n    {\\n      \\\"language_code\\\": \\\"en\\\",\\n      \\\"language_name\\\": \\\"English\\\",\\n      \\\"is_generated\\\": false,\\n      \\\"is_translatable\\\": true\\n    },\\n    {\\n      \\\"language_code\\\": \\\"en\\\",\\n      \\\"language_name\\\": \\\"English (auto-generated)\\\",\\n      \\\"is_generated\\\": true,\\n      \\\"is_translatable\\\": false\\n    },\\n    {\\n      \\\"language_code\\\": \\\"ru\\\",\\n      \\\"language_name\\\": \\\"Russian\\\",\\n      \\\"is_generated\\\": false,\\n      \\\"is_translatable\\\": true\\n    }\\n  ]\\n}\\n```\\n\\n**Implementation:**\\n```python\\n# backend/app/routers/transcripts.py (NEW FILE)\\nfrom fastapi import APIRouter, HTTPException, Query\\nfrom youtube_transcript_api import YouTubeTranscriptApi\\n\\nrouter = APIRouter()\\n\\n@router.get(\\\"/transcripts/list\\\")\\nasync def list_transcripts(url: str = Query(...)):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Get list of available transcripts for a YouTube video.\\n    Does not download transcript text - only metadata.\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    try:\\n        video_id = extract_video_id(url)\\n        \\n        # Use proxy for listing (same as extraction)\\n        proxy_config = get_proxy_config()\\n        ytt_api = YouTubeTranscriptApi(proxy_config=proxy_config)\\n        transcript_list = ytt_api.list_transcripts(video_id)\\n        \\n        available = []\\n        \\n        # Manual transcripts\\n        for transcript in transcript_list:\\n            if not transcript.is_generated:\\n                available.append({\\n                    \\\"language_code\\\": transcript.language_code,\\n                    \\\"language_name\\\": transcript.language,\\n                    \\\"is_generated\\\": False,\\n                    \\\"is_translatable\\\": transcript.is_translatable\\n                })\\n        \\n        # Auto-generated transcripts\\n        for transcript in transcript_list:\\n            if transcript.is_generated:\\n                available.append({\\n                    \\\"language_code\\\": transcript.language_code,\\n                    \\\"language_name\\\": f\\\"{transcript.language} (auto-generated)\\\",\\n                    \\\"is_generated\\\": True,\\n                    \\\"is_translatable\\\": transcript.is_translatable\\n                })\\n        \\n        return {\\n            \\\"video_id\\\": video_id,\\n            \\\"video_url\\\": url,\\n            \\\"available_transcripts\\\": available\\n        }\\n    \\n    except TranscriptsDisabled:\\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail=\\\"This video has no transcripts available.\\\")\\n    except Exception as e:\\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=str(e))\\n```\\n\\n### **2. Update POST /api/extract**\\n\\nAdd optional parameters: `language` and `prefer_manual`\\n\\n**New Request Schema:**\\n```python\\n# backend/app/models/schemas.py\\nclass ExtractRequest(BaseModel):\\n    url: str\\n    language: Optional[str] = None  # e.g., \\\"en\\\", \\\"ru\\\"\\n    prefer_manual: bool = True  # If true, prefer manual over auto-generated\\n```\\n\\n**Updated Logic:**\\n```python\\n# backend/app/services/extractors/youtube.py\\ndef extract_transcript(\\n    self, \\n    url: str, \\n    language: Optional[str] = None,\\n    prefer_manual: bool = True\\n) -> str:\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Extract transcript with language and type selection.\\n    \\n    Args:\\n        url: YouTube video URL\\n        language: Language code (e.g., \\\"en\\\", \\\"ru\\\"). If None, uses first available.\\n        prefer_manual: If True, prefer manual transcripts over auto-generated.\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    video_id = self._extract_video_id(url)\\n    \\n    for attempt in range(self.MAX_PROXY_RETRIES):\\n        try:\\n            proxy_config = self._get_proxy_config()\\n            ytt_api = YouTubeTranscriptApi(proxy_config=proxy_config)\\n            transcript_list = ytt_api.list_transcripts(video_id)\\n            \\n            # Find matching transcript\\n            if language:\\n                # User specified language\\n                if prefer_manual:\\n                    try:\\n                        transcript = transcript_list.find_transcript([language])\\n                        if not transcript.is_generated:\\n                            text = \\\" \\\".join(snippet['text'] for snippet in transcript.fetch())\\n                            return text\\n                    except:\\n                        pass\\n                \\n                # Try auto-generated\\n                try:\\n                    transcript = transcript_list.find_generated_transcript([language])\\n                    text = \\\" \\\".join(snippet['text'] for snippet in transcript.fetch())\\n                    return text\\n                except:\\n                    raise ValueError(f\\\"No transcript found for language: {language}\\\")\\n            else:\\n                # Auto-select: prefer manual, fallback to auto\\n                try:\\n                    transcript = transcript_list.find_transcript(['en', 'ru'])\\n                    text = \\\" \\\".join(snippet['text'] for snippet in transcript.fetch())\\n                    return text\\n                except:\\n                    transcript = transcript_list.find_generated_transcript(['en', 'ru'])\\n                    text = \\\" \\\".join(snippet['text'] for snippet in transcript.fetch())\\n                    return text\\n        \\n        except (TranscriptsDisabled, NoTranscriptFound) as e:\\n            raise ValueError(str(e))\\n        except Exception as exc:\\n            last_exception = exc\\n            logger.warning(f\\\"Attempt {attempt + 1} failed: {exc}\\\")\\n    \\n    raise RuntimeError(f\\\"Failed after retries. Last error: {last_exception}\\\")\\n```\\n\\n### **3. Update Router Registration**\\n\\n```python\\n# backend/main.py\\nfrom app.routers import extract, transcripts\\n\\napp.include_router(extract.router, prefix=\\\"/api\\\", tags=[\\\"extract\\\"])\\napp.include_router(transcripts.router, prefix=\\\"/api\\\", tags=[\\\"transcripts\\\"])  # NEW\\n```\\n\\n---\\n\\n## 🎨 Frontend Implementation\\n\\n### **1. Update Dashboard Page**\\n\\n**UI Flow:**\\n\\n```\\n[YouTube URL Input]\\n         ↓\\n    [Analyze Button]\\n         ↓\\n   (Loading spinner)\\n         ↓\\n[Transcript Options Dropdown] ← Only if >1 option\\n  - English (manual)\\n  - English (auto-generated)\\n  - Russian\\n         ↓\\n    [Extract Button]\\n         ↓\\n   (Show transcript)\\n```\\n\\n### **2. Component: TranscriptSelector**\\n\\n```typescript\\n// frontend/src/components/TranscriptSelector.tsx (NEW FILE)\\n\\ninterface TranscriptOption {\\n  language_code: string;\\n  language_name: string;\\n  is_generated: boolean;\\n  is_translatable: boolean;\\n}\\n\\ninterface TranscriptSelectorProps {\\n  url: string;\\n  onSelect: (language: string, isGenerated: boolean) => void;\\n}\\n\\nexport function TranscriptSelector({ url, onSelect }: TranscriptSelectorProps) {\\n  const [options, setOptions] = useState<TranscriptOption[]>([]);\\n  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);\\n  const [selected, setSelected] = useState<TranscriptOption | null>(null);\\n\\n  const fetchOptions = async () => {\\n    setLoading(true);\\n    try {\\n      const response = await fetch(\\n        `${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL}/api/transcripts/list?url=${encodeURIComponent(url)}`\\n      );\\n      const data = await response.json();\\n      setOptions(data.available_transcripts);\\n      \\n      // Auto-select first option if only one available\\n      if (data.available_transcripts.length === 1) {\\n        const option = data.available_transcripts[0];\\n        setSelected(option);\\n        onSelect(option.language_code, option.is_generated);\\n      }\\n    } catch (error) {\\n      console.error('Failed to fetch transcript options:', error);\\n    } finally {\\n      setLoading(false);\\n    }\\n  };\\n\\n  const handleSelect = (option: TranscriptOption) => {\\n    setSelected(option);\\n    onSelect(option.language_code, option.is_generated);\\n  };\\n\\n  return (\\n    <div>\\n      <button onClick={fetchOptions} disabled={loading}>\\n        {loading ? 'Analyzing...' : 'Analyze Video'}\\n      </button>\\n\\n      {options.length > 1 && (\\n        <select onChange={(e) => {\\n          const option = options.find(o => o.language_code === e.target.value);\\n          if (option) handleSelect(option);\\n        }}>\\n          <option value=\\\"\\\">Select language...</option>\\n          {options.map((option, idx) => (\\n            <option key={idx} value={option.language_code}>\\n              {option.language_name}\\n            </option>\\n          ))}\\n        </select>\\n      )}\\n\\n      {selected && (\\n        <p>Selected: {selected.language_name}</p>\\n      )}\\n    </div>\\n  );\\n}\\n```\\n\\n### **3. Update Dashboard to Use TranscriptSelector**\\n\\n```typescript\\n// frontend/src/app/dashboard/page.tsx\\n\\nconst [selectedLanguage, setSelectedLanguage] = useState<string | null>(null);\\nconst [preferManual, setPreferManual] = useState(true);\\n\\nconst handleExtract = async () => {\\n  const response = await fetch(`${API_URL}/api/extract`, {\\n    method: 'POST',\\n    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\\n    body: JSON.stringify({\\n      url: videoUrl,\\n      language: selectedLanguage,\\n      prefer_manual: preferManual\\n    })\\n  });\\n  // ... handle response\\n};\\n\\nreturn (\\n  <>\\n    <input \\n      value={videoUrl} \\n      onChange={(e) => setVideoUrl(e.target.value)} \\n      placeholder=\\\"YouTube URL\\\"\\n    />\\n    \\n    <TranscriptSelector \\n      url={videoUrl}\\n      onSelect={(lang, isGenerated) => {\\n        setSelectedLanguage(lang);\\n        setPreferManual(!isGenerated);\\n      }}\\n    />\\n    \\n    <button onClick={handleExtract}>Extract Transcript</button>\\n  </>\\n);\\n```\\n\\n---\\n\\n## 📋 Files to Create/Modify\\n\\n### **Backend:**\\n\\n**New Files:**\\n- `backend/app/routers/transcripts.py` - This leads to errors like \\\"Transcripts are disabled\\\" even when auto-generated subtitles exist.\\n\\nUsers have no control over:\\n- Which language to use (if multiple available)\\n- Manual vs auto-generated subtitles\\n\\n## Solution\\n\\nImplement **two-step flow**:\\n\\n### **Step 1: List Available Transcripts**\\nUser enters URL → Backend returns list of available transcripts (without downloading)\\n\\n### **Step 2: Extract Selected Transcript**\\nUser selects language + type → Backend downloads chosen transcript\\n\\n---\\n\\n## 📦 Backend Implementation\\n\\n### **1. New Endpoint: GET /api/transcripts/list**\\n\\n**Request:**\\n```\\nGET /api/transcripts/list?url=https://youtube.com/watch?v=VIDEO_ID\\n```\\n\\n**Response:**\\n```json\\n{\\n  \\\"video_id\\\": \\\"L-BgxLtMxh0\\\",\\n  \\\"video_url\\\": \\\"https://youtube.com/watch?v=L-BgxLtMxh0\\\",\\n  \\\"available_transcripts\\\": [\\n    {\\n      \\\"language_code\\\": \\\"en\\\",\\n      \\\"language_name\\\": \\\"English\\\",\\n      \\\"is_generated\\\": false,\\n      \\\"is_translatable\\\": true\\n    },\\n    {\\n      \\\"language_code\\\": \\\"en\\\",\\n      \\\"language_name\\\": \\\"English (auto-generated)\\\",\\n      \\\"is_generated\\\": true,\\n      \\\"is_translatable\\\": false\\n    },\\n    {\\n      \\\"language_code\\\": \\\"ru\\\",\\n      \\\"language_name\\\": \\\"Russian\\\",\\n      \\\"is_generated\\\": false,\\n      \\\"is_translatable\\\": true\\n    }\\n  ]\\n}\\n```\\n\\n**Implementation:**\\n```python\\n# backend/app/routers/transcripts.py (NEW FILE)\\nfrom fastapi import APIRouter, HTTPException, Query\\nfrom youtube_transcript_api import YouTubeTranscriptApi\\n\\nrouter = APIRouter()\\n\\n@router.get(\\\"/transcripts/list\\\")\\nasync def list_transcripts(url: str = Query(...)):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Get list of available transcripts for a YouTube video.\\n    Does not download transcript text - only metadata.\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    try:\\n        video_id = extract_video_id(url)\\n        \\n        # Use proxy for listing (same as extraction)\\n        proxy_config = get_proxy_config()\\n        ytt_api = YouTubeTranscriptApi(proxy_config=proxy_config)\\n        transcript_list = ytt_api.list_transcripts(video_id)\\n        \\n        available = []\\n        \\n        # Manual transcripts\\n        for transcript in transcript_list:\\n            if not transcript.is_generated:\\n                available.append({\\n                    \\\"language_code\\\": transcript.language_code,\\n                    \\\"language_name\\\": transcript.language,\\n                    \\\"is_generated\\\": False,\\n                    \\\"is_translatable\\\": transcript.is_translatable\\n                })\\n        \\n        # Auto-generated transcripts\\n        for transcript in transcript_list:\\n            if transcript.is_generated:\\n                available.append({\\n                    \\\"language_code\\\": transcript.language_code,\\n                    \\\"language_name\\\": f\\\"{transcript.language} (auto-generated)\\\",\\n                    \\\"is_generated\\\": True,\\n                    \\\"is_translatable\\\": transcript.is_translatable\\n                })\\n        \\n        return {\\n            \\\"video_id\\\": video_id,\\n            \\\"video_url\\\": url,\\n            \\\"available_transcripts\\\": available\\n        }\\n    \\n    except TranscriptsDisabled:\\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail=\\\"This video has no transcripts available.\\\")\\n    except Exception as e:\\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=str(e))\\n```\\n\\n### **2. If None, uses first available.\\n        prefer_manual: If True, prefer manual transcripts over auto-generated.\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    video_id = self._extract_video_id(url)\\n    \\n    for attempt in range(self.MAX_PROXY_RETRIES):\\n        try:\\n            proxy_config = self._get_proxy_config()\\n            ytt_api = YouTubeTranscriptApi(proxy_config=proxy_config)\\n            transcript_list = ytt_api.list_transcripts(video_id)\\n            \\n            # Find matching transcript\\n            if language:\\n                # User specified language\\n                if prefer_manual:\\n                    try:\\n                        transcript = transcript_list.find_transcript([language])\\n                        if not transcript.is_generated:\\n                            text = \\\" \\\".join(snippet['text'] for snippet in transcript.fetch())\\n                            return text\\n                    except:\\n                        pass\\n                \\n                # Try auto-generated\\n                try:\\n                    transcript = transcript_list.find_generated_transcript([language])\\n                    text = \\\" \\\".join(snippet['text'] for snippet in transcript.fetch())\\n                    return text\\n                except:\\n                    raise ValueError(f\\\"No transcript found for language: {language}\\\")\\n            else:\\n                # Auto-select: prefer manual, fallback to auto\\n                try:\\n                    transcript = transcript_list.find_transcript(['en', 'ru'])\\n                    text = \\\" \\\".join(snippet['text'] for snippet in transcript.fetch())\\n                    return text\\n                except:\\n                    transcript = transcript_list.find_generated_transcript(['en', 'ru'])\\n                    text = \\\" \\\".join(snippet['text'] for snippet in transcript.fetch())\\n                    return text\\n        \\n        except (TranscriptsDisabled, NoTranscriptFound) as e:\\n            raise ValueError(str(e))\\n        except Exception as exc:\\n            last_exception = exc\\n            logger.warning(f\\\"Attempt {attempt + 1} failed: {exc}\\\")\\n    \\n    raise RuntimeError(f\\\"Failed after retries. Last error: {last_exception}\\\")\\n```\\n\\n### **3. Update Dashboard Page**\\n\\n**UI Flow:**\\n\\n```\\n[YouTube URL Input]\\n         ↓\\n    [Analyze Button]\\n         ↓\\n   (Loading spinner)\\n         ↓\\n[Transcript Options Dropdown] ← Only if >1 option\\n  - English (manual)\\n  - English (auto-generated)\\n  - Russian\\n         ↓\\n    [Extract Button]\\n         ↓\\n   (Show transcript)\\n```\\n\\n### **2. Component: TranscriptSelector**\\n\\n```typescript\\n// frontend/src/components/TranscriptSelector.tsx (NEW FILE)\\n\\ninterface TranscriptOption {\\n  language_code: string;\\n  language_name: string;\\n  is_generated: boolean;\\n  is_translatable: boolean;\\n}\\n\\ninterface TranscriptSelectorProps {\\n  url: string;\\n  onSelect: (language: string, isGenerated: boolean) => void;\\n}\\n\\nexport function TranscriptSelector({ url, onSelect }: TranscriptSelectorProps) {\\n  const [options, setOptions] = useState<TranscriptOption[]>([]);\\n  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);\\n  const [selected, setSelected] = useState<TranscriptOption | null>(null);\\n\\n  const fetchOptions = async () => {\\n    setLoading(true);\\n    try {\\n      const response = await fetch(\\n        `${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL}/api/transcripts/list?url=${encodeURIComponent(url)}`\\n      );\\n      const data = await response.json();\\n      setOptions(data.available_transcripts);\\n      \\n      // Auto-select first option if only one available\\n      if (data.available_transcripts.length === 1) {\\n        const option = data.available_transcripts[0];\\n        setSelected(option);\\n        onSelect(option.language_code, option.is_generated);\\n      }\\n    } catch (error) {\\n      console.error('Failed to fetch transcript options:', error);\\n    } finally {\\n      setLoading(false);\\n    }\\n  };\\n\\n  const handleSelect = (option: TranscriptOption) => {\\n    setSelected(option);\\n    onSelect(option.language_code, option.is_generated);\\n  };\\n\\n  return (\\n    <div>\\n      <button onClick={fetchOptions} disabled={loading}>\\n        {loading ? 'Analyzing...' : 'Analyze Video'}\\n      </button>\\n\\n      {options.length > 1 && (\\n        <select onChange={(e) => {\\n          const option = options.find(o => o.language_code === e.target.value);\\n          if (option) handleSelect(option);\\n        }}>\\n          <option value=\\\"\\\">Select language...</option>\\n          {options.map((option, idx) => (\\n            <option key={idx} value={option.language_code}>\\n              {option.language_name}\\n            </option>\\n          ))}\\n        </select>\\n      )}\\n\\n      {selected && (\\n        <p>Selected: {selected.language_name}</p>\\n      )}\\n    </div>\\n  );\\n}\\n```\\n\\n### **3. Update Dashboard to Use TranscriptSelector**\\n\\n```typescript\\n// frontend/src/app/dashboard/page.tsx\\n\\nconst [selectedLanguage, setSelectedLanguage] = useState<string | null>(null);\\nconst [preferManual, setPreferManual] = useState(true);\\n\\nconst handleExtract = async () => {\\n  const response = await fetch(`${API_URL}/api/extract`, {\\n    method: 'POST',\\n    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\\n    body: JSON.stringify({\\n      url: videoUrl,\\n      language: selectedLanguage,\\n      prefer_manual: preferManual\\n    })\\n  });\\n  // ... handle response\\n};\\n\\nreturn (\\n  <>\\n    <input \\n      value={videoUrl} \\n      onChange={(e) => setVideoUrl(e.target.value)} \\n      placeholder=\\\"YouTube URL\\\"\\n    />\\n    \\n    <TranscriptSelector \\n      url={videoUrl}\\n      onSelect={(lang, isGenerated) => {\\n        setSelectedLanguage(lang);\\n        setPreferManual(!isGenerated);\\n      }}\\n    />\\n    \\n    <button onClick={handleExtract}>Extract Transcript</button>\\n  </>\\n);\\n```\\n\\n---\\n\\n## 📋 Files to Create/Modify\\n\\n### **Backend:**\\n\\n**New Files:**\\n- `backend/app/routers/transcripts.py` - ❌ No such method!\\n```\\n\\n**Correct usage:**\\n```python\\ntranscript_list = YouTubeTranscriptApi.list_transcripts(\\n    video_id,\\n    proxies=proxies_dict  # Must be dict, not GenericProxyConfig\\n)\\n```\\n\\n## Additional Issue\\n\\n`list_transcripts()` expects `proxies` as a **dictionary**, not `GenericProxyConfig`.\\n\\n**Format:**\\n```python\\nproxies = {\\n    'http': 'http://user:pass@host:port',\\n    'https': 'http://user:pass@host:port'\\n}\\n```\\n\\n---\\n\\n## 🔧 Solution\\n\\n### Fix 1: Update `backend/app/routers/transcripts.py`\\n\\nReplace:\\n```python\\nproxy_config = get_proxy_config()\\nytt_api = YouTubeTranscriptApi(proxy_config=proxy_config)\\ntranscript_list = ytt_api.list_transcripts(video_id)\\n```\\n\\nWith:\\n```python\\nproxies = get_proxy_dict()  # Returns dict, not GenericProxyConfig\\ntranscript_list = YouTubeTranscriptApi.list_transcripts(video_id, proxies=proxies)\\n```\\n\\n### Fix 2: Update `backend/app/services/extractors/youtube.py`\\n\\n**Add helper method to get proxies as dict:**\\n```python\\ndef _get_proxy_dict(self) -> dict | None:\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Returns proxy configuration as dict for youtube-transcript-api.\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    if self._rotating_proxy_configured():\\n        proxy_url = self._get_random_proxy()\\n        return {\\n            'http': proxy_url,\\n            'https': proxy_url\\n        }\\n    \\n    if self._legacy_proxy_list:\\n        proxy_url = random.choice(self._legacy_proxy_list)\\n        return {\\n            'http': proxy_url,\\n            'https': proxy_url\\n        }\\n    \\n    return None\\n```\\n\\n**Update `extract_transcript()` method:**\\n```python\\ndef extract_transcript(\\n    self, \\n    url: str, \\n    language: Optional[str] = None,\\n    prefer_manual: bool = True\\n) -> str:\\n    video_id = self._extract_video_id(url)\\n    \\n    for attempt in range(self.MAX_PROXY_RETRIES):\\n        try:\\n            proxies = self._get_proxy_dict()\\n            \\n            # Use static method with proxies dict\\n            transcript_list = YouTubeTranscriptApi.list_transcripts(\\n                video_id, \\n                proxies=proxies\\n            )\\n            \\n            # Find and fetch transcript based on user preferences\\n            transcript = None\\n            \\n            if language:\\n                # User specified language\\n                if prefer_manual:\\n                    # Try manual first\\n                    try:\\n                        for t in transcript_list:\\n                            if t.language_code == language and not t.is_generated:\\n                                transcript = t\\n                                break\\n                    except:\\n                        pass\\n                \\n                # Fallback to auto-generated\\n                if not transcript:\\n                    for t in transcript_list:\\n                        if t.language_code == language and t.is_generated:\\n                            transcript = t\\n                            break\\n                \\n                if not transcript:\\n                    raise ValueError(f\\\"No transcript found for language: {language}\\\")\\n            else:\\n                # Auto-select: prefer manual en/ru, fallback to auto-generated\\n                for lang in ['en', 'ru']:\\n                    for t in transcript_list:\\n                        if t.language_code == lang and not t.is_generated:\\n                            transcript = t\\n                            break\\n                    if transcript:\\n                        break\\n                \\n                # Fallback to auto-generated\\n                if not transcript:\\n                    for lang in ['en', 'ru']:\\n                        for t in transcript_list:\\n                            if t.language_code == lang and t.is_generated:\\n                                transcript = t\\n                                break\\n                        if transcript:\\n                            break\\n                \\n                if not transcript:\\n                    raise ValueError(\\\"No transcript found in English or Russian\\\")\\n            \\n            # Fetch transcript text\\n            transcript_data = transcript.fetch()\\n            text = \\\" \\\".join(item['text'] for item in transcript_data)\\n            \\n            logger.info(\\n                \\\"Successfully extracted %s transcript for %s (attempt %d)\\\",\\n                \\\"manual\\\" if not transcript.is_generated else \\\"auto-generated\\\",\\n                video_id,\\n                attempt + 1\\n            )\\n            return text\\n        \\n        except TranscriptsDisabled:\\n            raise ValueError(\\\"Transcripts are disabled for this video.\\\")\\n        \\n        except NoTranscriptFound:\\n            raise ValueError(\\\"No transcript found for this video.\\\")\\n        \\n        except Exception as exc:\\n            last_exception = exc\\n            logger.warning(\\\"Attempt %d failed: %s\\\", attempt + 1, exc)\\n    \\n    error_msg = f\\\"Failed to extract transcript after {self.MAX_PROXY_RETRIES} attempt(s).\\\"\\n    error_msg += \\\" All proxies failed. YouTube may be blocking these IPs.\\\"\\n    raise RuntimeError(f\\\"{error_msg} Last error: {last_exception}\\\") from last_exception\\n```\\n\\n### Fix 3: Update `backend/app/routers/transcripts.py`\\n\\n```python\\nfrom fastapi import APIRouter, HTTPException, Query\\nfrom youtube_transcript_api import YouTubeTranscriptApi\\nfrom youtube_transcript_api._errors import TranscriptsDisabled, NoTranscriptFound\\nfrom app.services.extractors.youtube import YouTubeExtractor\\nimport logging\\n\\nlogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)\\nrouter = APIRouter()\\n\\n@router.get(\\\"/transcripts/list\\\")\\nasync def list_transcripts(url: str = Query(...)):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Get list of available transcripts for a YouTube video.\\n    Does not download transcript text - only metadata.\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    extractor = YouTubeExtractor()\\n    \\n    try:\\n        video_id = extractor.get_video_id(url)\\n        \\n        # Get proxy as dict (not GenericProxyConfig)\\n        proxies = extractor._get_proxy_dict()\\n        \\n        # Use static method\\n        transcript_list = YouTubeTranscriptApi.list_transcripts(\\n            video_id, \\n            proxies=proxies\\n        )\\n        \\n        available = []\\n        \\n        # Collect manual transcripts\\n        for transcript in transcript_list:\\n            if not transcript.is_generated:\\n                available.append({\\n                    \\\"language_code\\\": transcript.language_code,\\n                    \\\"language_name\\\": transcript.language,\\n                    \\\"is_generated\\\": False,\\n                    \\\"is_translatable\\\": transcript.is_translatable\\n                })\\n        \\n        # Collect auto-generated transcripts\\n        for transcript in transcript_list:\\n            if transcript.is_generated:\\n                available.append({\\n                    \\\"language_code\\\": transcript.language_code,\\n                    \\\"language_name\\\": f\\\"{transcript.language} (auto-generated)\\\",\\n                    \\\"is_generated\\\": True,\\n                    \\\"is_translatable\\\": transcript.is_translatable\\n                })\\n        \\n        logger.info(\\\"Found %d transcript options for video %s\\\", len(available), video_id)\\n        \\n        return {\\n            \\\"video_id\\\": video_id,\\n            \\\"video_url\\\": url,\\n            \\\"available_transcripts\\\": available\\n        }\\n    \\n    except TranscriptsDisabled:\\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail=\\\"This video has no transcripts available.\\\")\\n    except NoTranscriptFound:\\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail=\\\"No transcripts found for this video.\\\")\\n    except Exception as e:\\n        logger.error(\\\"Failed to list transcripts: %s\\\", str(e))\\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=f\\\"Failed to list transcripts: {str(e)}\\\")\\n```\\n\\n---\\n\\n## 📋 Files to Modify\\n\\n- `backend/app/services/extractors/youtube.py` - Add `_get_proxy_dict()`, fix `extract_transcript()`\\n- `backend/app/routers/transcripts.py` - Fix `list_transcripts` endpoint to use static method\\n\\n---\\n\\n## ✅ Testing\\n\\nAfter fix:\\n1. `GET /api/transcripts/list?url=https://youtube.com/watch?v=VIDEO_ID` should return list\\n2. `POST /api/extract` with language selection should work\\n3. Separately, the frontend components were calling `/extract` and `/generate` without the `/api` prefix that the FastAPI routers require.\n\n## Backend (`youtube.py`)\n- Replace static `YouTubeTranscriptApi.get_transcript(video_id)` with instance-based `YouTubeTranscriptApi().fetch(video_id)`\n- Update snippet text access from dict key `entry[\"text\"]` to dataclass attribute `snippet.text` (`FetchedTranscript` yields `FetchedTranscriptSnippet` objects)\n\n```python\n# Before (broken with >=1.2.0)\ntranscript_list = YouTubeTranscriptApi.get_transcript(video_id)\ntext = \" \".join(entry[\"text\"] for entry in transcript_list)\n\n# After\nytt_api = YouTubeTranscriptApi()\ntranscript = ytt_api.fetch(video_id)\ntext = \" \".join(snippet.text for snippet in transcript)\n```\n\n## Frontend (`UrlInput.tsx`, `Dashboard.tsx`)\n- `UrlInput.tsx`: `/extract` → `/api/extract`\n- `Dashboard.tsx`: `/generate` → `/api/generate`\n\nThese components were bypassing the shared `api.ts` module (which already had correct paths) and constructing URLs inline without the required prefix.\n\n<!-- START COPILOT ORIGINAL PROMPT -->\n\n\n\n<details>\n\n<summary>Original prompt</summary>\n\n## Problem\n\nYouTube transcript extraction is completely broken due to two issues:\n\n### 1. `youtube-transcript-api` breaking change (critical)\n\nThe library removed the old static methods (`YouTubeTranscriptApi.get_transcript()`) in v1.2.0 (July 2025). The current installed version is 1.2.4, but the backend code still uses the deleted API.\n\n**Current broken code** in `backend/app/services/extractors/youtube.py`:\n```python\nfrom youtube_transcript_api import YouTubeTranscriptApi\ntranscript_list = YouTubeTranscriptApi.get_transcript(video_id)\n```\n\n**Must migrate to the new API:**\n```python\nfrom youtube_transcript_api import YouTubeTranscriptApi\nytt_api = YouTubeTranscriptApi()\ntranscript = ytt_api.fetch(video_id)\n```\n\nThe new `fetch()` returns a `FetchedTranscript` object (iterable, indexable). Each snippet has `.text`, `.start`, `.duration` attributes instead of dict keys. Use `.to_raw_data()` if you need list-of-dicts format.\n\nAlso update exception imports — the old exception names may have changed. Check the library's current exception classes.\n\n### 2. Frontend URL paths missing `/api` prefix\n\nThe backend mounts routers with `prefix=\"/api\"`:\n```python\napp.include_router(extract.router, prefix=\"/api\")\napp.include_router(generate.router, prefix=\"/api\")\n```\n\nBut the frontend components `UrlInput.tsx` and `Dashboard.tsx` call the API **without** the `/api` prefix:\n\n- `frontend/src/components/dashboard/UrlInput.tsx` calls `${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL}/extract` — should be `/api/extract`\n- `frontend/src/components/dashboard/Dashboard.tsx` calls `${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL}/generate` — should be `/api/generate`\n\nMeanwhile, `frontend/src/lib/api.ts` correctly uses `/api/extract` and `/api/generate`, but the components don't use this shared module.\n\n## What to fix\n\n1. **`backend/app/services/extractors/youtube.py`** — Migrate from `YouTubeTranscriptApi.get_transcript(video_id)` to `YouTubeTranscriptApi().fetch(video_id)`. Update the transcript text joining logic to work with the new `FetchedTranscript` object. Update exception handling to use current exception class names from the library.\n\n2. **`frontend/src/components/dashboard/UrlInput.tsx`** — Fix the fetch URL from `${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL}/extract` to `${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL}/api/extract`.\n\n3. **`frontend/src/components/dashboard/Dashboard.tsx`** — Fix the fetch URL from `${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL}/generate` to `${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL}/api/generate`.\n\n4. The current installed version is 1.2.4, but the backend code still uses the deleted API.\n\n**Current broken code** in `backend/app/services/extractors/youtube.py`:\n```python\nfrom youtube_transcript_api import YouTubeTranscriptApi\ntranscript_list = YouTubeTranscriptApi.get_transcript(video_id)\n```\n\n**Must migrate to the new API:**\n```python\nfrom youtube_transcript_api import YouTubeTranscriptApi\nytt_api = YouTubeTranscriptApi()\ntranscript = ytt_api.fetch(video_id)\n```\n\nThe new `fetch()` returns a `FetchedTranscript` object (iterable, indexable). Each snippet has `.text`, `.start`, `.duration` attributes instead of dict keys. Use `.to_raw_data()` if you need list-of-dicts format.\n\nAlso update exception imports — the old exception names may have changed. Check the library's current exception classes.\n\n### 2. Each snippet has `.text`, `.start`, `.duration` attributes instead of dict keys. The current installed version is 1.2.4, but the backend code still uses the deleted API.\n\n**Current broken code** in `backend/app/services/extractors/youtube.py`:\n```python\nfrom youtube_transcript_api import YouTubeTranscriptApi\ntranscript_list = YouTubeTranscriptApi.get_transcript(video_id)\n```\n\n**Must migrate to the new API:**\n```python\nfrom youtube_transcript_api import YouTubeTranscriptApi\nytt_api = YouTubeTranscriptApi()\ntranscript = ytt_api.fetch(video_id)\n```\n\nThe new `fetch()` returns a `FetchedTranscript` object (iterable, indexable). Each snippet has `.text`, `.start`, `.duration` attributes instead of dict keys. Use `.to_raw_data()` if you need list-of-dicts format.\n\nAlso update exception imports — the old exception names may have changed. Check the library's current exception classes.\n\n### 2. Frontend URL paths missing `/api` prefix\n\nThe backend mounts routers with `prefix=\"/api\"`:\n```python\napp.include_router(extract.router, prefix=\"/api\")\napp.include_router(generate.router, prefix=\"/api\")\n```\n\nBut the frontend components `UrlInput.tsx` and `Dashboard.tsx` call the API **without** the `/api` prefix:\n\n- `frontend/src/components/dashboard/UrlInput.tsx` calls `${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL}/extract` — should be `/api/extract`\n- `frontend/src/components/dashboard/Dashboard.tsx` calls `${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL}/generate` — should be `/api/generate`\n\nMeanwhile, `frontend/src/lib/api.ts` correctly uses `/api/extract` and `/api/generate`, but the components don't use this shared module.\n\n## What to fix\n\n1. **`backend/app/services/extractors/youtube.py`** — Migrate from `YouTubeTranscriptApi.get_transcript(video_id)` to `YouTubeTranscriptApi().fetch(video_id)`. Update the transcript text joining logic to work with the new `FetchedTranscript` object. Each snippet has `.text`, `.start`, `.duration` attributes instead of dict keys. Each snippet has `.text`, `.start`, `.duration` attributes instead of dict keys. Use `.to_raw_data()` if you need list-of-dicts format.\n\nAlso update exception imports — the old exception names may have changed. Check the library's current exception classes.\n\n### 2. Find best matching subtitle\\n                for lang in lang_candidates:\\n                    if prefer_manual and lang in subtitles:\\n                        return self._download_subtitle(subtitles[lang])\\n                    elif lang in automatic_captions:\\n                        return self._download_subtitle(automatic_captions[lang])\\n                \\n                # Fallback: try opposite preference\\n                for lang in lang_candidates:\\n                    if not prefer_manual and lang in subtitles:\\n                        return self._download_subtitle(subtitles[lang])\\n                \\n                raise ValueError(f\\\"No transcript found for language(s): {', '.join(lang_candidates)}\\\")\\n        \\n        except ValueError:\\n            raise\\n        except Exception as exc:\\n            last_exception = exc\\n            logger.warning(\\\"Attempt %d failed: %s\\\", attempt + 1, exc)\\n    \\n    raise RuntimeError(f\\\"Failed to extract transcript after {self.MAX_PROXY_RETRIES} attempts. Even with valid proxies, the library fails to parse responses.\\n\\n## Solution\\n\\nMigrate to **`yt-dlp`** — the industry-standard YouTube downloader that:\\n- ✅ Constantly updated to bypass YouTube changes (active in 2026)\\n- ✅ Built-in proxy support with automatic rotation\\n- ✅ Handles rate limiting and IP blocks\\n- ✅ Extracts subtitles (manual + auto-generated)\\n- ✅ Production-ready, used by millions\\n\\n---\\n\\n## 📦 Changes Required\\n\\n### **1. Fallback: try opposite preference\\n                for lang in lang_candidates:\\n                    if not prefer_manual and lang in subtitles:\\n                        return self._download_subtitle(subtitles[lang])\\n                \\n                raise ValueError(f\\\"No transcript found for language(s): {', '.join(lang_candidates)}\\\")\\n        \\n        except ValueError:\\n            raise\\n        except Exception as exc:\\n            last_exception = exc\\n            logger.warning(\\\"Attempt %d failed: %s\\\", attempt + 1, exc)\\n    \\n    raise RuntimeError(f\\\"Failed to extract transcript after {self.MAX_PROXY_RETRIES} attempts. Get cookies through proxy if configured\\n            proxy_url = None\\n            if self._rotating_proxy_configured():\\n                proxy_url = self._get_random_proxy()\\n            elif self._legacy_proxy_list:\\n                proxy_url = random.choice(self._legacy_proxy_list)\\n                logger.info(\\\"Using static proxy from list\\\")\\n            \\n            if proxy_url:\\n                cookie_file_path = self._get_youtube_cookies_via_proxy(video_id, proxy_url)\\n            \\n            # Configure yt-dlp with cookies (no direct proxy)\\n            ydl_opts = {\\n                'skip_download': True,\\n                'quiet': True,\\n                'no_warnings': True,\\n                'extract_flat': False,\\n            }\\n            \\n            if cookie_file_path:\\n                ydl_opts['cookiefile'] = cookie_file_path\\n            \\n            with yt_dlp.YoutubeDL(ydl_opts) as ydl:\\n                info = ydl.extract_info(f'https://youtube.com/watch?v={video_id}', download=False)\\n                \\n                if not info:\\n                    raise ValueError(\\\"Could not extract video information\\\")\\n                \\n                subtitles = info.get('subtitles', {})\\n                automatic_captions = info.get('automatic_captions', {})\\n                \\n                available = []\\n                \\n                # Manual subtitles first\\n                for lang_code in subtitles.keys():\\n                    available.append({\\n                        \\\"language_code\\\": lang_code,\\n                        \\\"language_name\\\": self._get_language_name(lang_code),\\n                        \\\"is_generated\\\": False,\\n                        \\\"is_translatable\\\": False,\\n                    })\\n                \\n                # Auto-generated subtitles second (only if not already in manual)\\n                for lang_code in automatic_captions.keys():\\n                    if lang_code not in subtitles:\\n                        available.append({\\n                            \\\"language_code\\\": lang_code,\\n                            \\\"language_name\\\": f\\\"{self._get_language_name(lang_code)} (auto-generated)\\\",\\n                            \\\"is_generated\\\": True,\\n                            \\\"is_translatable\\\": False,\\n                        })\\n                \\n                logger.info(\\\"Listed %d transcripts for %s\\\", len(available), video_id)\\n                return available\\n        \\n        except Exception as exc:\\n            last_exception = exc\\n            logger.warning(\\\"List attempt %d failed: %s\\\", attempt + 1, exc)\\n        \\n        finally:\\n            # Clean up temp cookie file\\n            if cookie_file_path and Path(cookie_file_path).exists():\\n                try:\\n                    Path(cookie_file_path).unlink()\\n                except Exception as cleanup_exc:\\n                    logger.warning(\\\"Failed to delete temp cookie file: %s\\\", cleanup_exc)\\n    \\n    error_msg = f\\\"Failed to list transcripts after {max_attempts} attempt(s).\\\"\\n    if proxy_active:\\n        error_msg += \\\" All proxies failed. YouTube is likely blocking your server IP.\\\"\\n    \\n    raise RuntimeError(f\\\"{error_msg} Last error: {last_exception}\\\") from last_exception\\n```\\n\\n**Update `extract_transcript()` method:**\\n```python\\ndef extract_transcript(\\n    self,\\n    url: str,\\n    language: str | None = None,\\n    prefer_manual: bool = True,\\n) -> str:\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Extract transcript from YouTube video.\\n    Uses proxy rotation with retry logic if proxies are configured.\\n    \\n    Args:\\n        url: YouTube video URL.\\n        language: YouTube language code (e.g. \\\"en\\\", \\\"ru\\\"). Get cookies through proxy if configured\\n            proxy_url = None\\n            if self._rotating_proxy_configured():\\n                proxy_url = self._get_random_proxy()\\n            elif self._legacy_proxy_list:\\n                proxy_url = random.choice(self._legacy_proxy_list)\\n                logger.info(\\\"Using static proxy from list\\\")\\n            \\n            if proxy_url:\\n                cookie_file_path = self._get_youtube_cookies_via_proxy(video_id, proxy_url)\\n            \\n            # Find best matching subtitle\\n                for lang in lang_candidates:\\n                    if prefer_manual and lang in subtitles:\\n                        text = self._download_and_parse_subtitle(subtitles[lang], proxy_url)\\n                        logger.info(\\\"Successfully extracted manual transcript for %s (attempt %d)\\\", video_id, attempt + 1)\\n                        return text\\n                    elif lang in automatic_captions:\\n                        text = self._download_and_parse_subtitle(automatic_captions[lang], proxy_url)\\n                        logger.info(\\\"Successfully extracted auto-generated transcript for %s (attempt %d)\\\", video_id, attempt + 1)\\n                        return text\\n                \\n                # Fallback: try opposite preference\\n                for lang in lang_candidates:\\n                    if not prefer_manual and lang in subtitles:\\n                        text = self._download_and_parse_subtitle(subtitles[lang], proxy_url)\\n                        logger.info(\\\"Successfully extracted manual transcript for %s (attempt %d)\\\", video_id, attempt + 1)\\n                        return text\\n                \\n                raise ValueError(f\\\"No transcript found for language(s): {', '.join(lang_candidates)}\\\")\\n        \\n        except ValueError:\\n            # Clean up temp cookie file\\n            if cookie_file_path and Path(cookie_file_path).exists():\\n                try:\\n                    Path(cookie_file_path).unlink()\\n                except Exception as cleanup_exc:\\n                    logger.warning(\\\"Failed to delete temp cookie file: %s\\\", cleanup_exc)\\n    \\n    error_msg = f\\\"Failed to extract transcript after {max_attempts} attempt(s).\\\"\\n    if proxy_active:\\n        error_msg += \\\" All proxies failed. YouTube is likely blocking your server IP.\\\"\\n    \\n    raise RuntimeError(f\\\"{error_msg} Last error: {last_exception}\\\") from last_exception\\n```\\n\\n**Add subtitle download helper:**\\n```python\\ndef _download_and_parse_subtitle(self, formats: list, proxy_url: str | None) -> str:\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Download and parse subtitle from the first available format.\\n    Uses proxy if provided.\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    for fmt in formats:\\n        if fmt.get('ext') in ['json3', 'srv3', 'vtt', 'srv1', 'srv2']:\\n            subtitle_url = fmt.get('url')\\n            if subtitle_url:\\n                try:\\n                    session = requests.Session()\\n                    if proxy_url:\\n                        session.proxies = {'http': proxy_url, 'https': proxy_url}\\n                    \\n                    response = session.get(subtitle_url, timeout=15)\\n                    response.raise_for_status()\\n                    \\n                    # Parse based on format\\n                    if fmt.get('ext') == 'json3':\\n                        return self._parse_json3_subtitle(response.text)\\n                    elif fmt.get('ext') == 'vtt':\\n                        return self._parse_vtt_subtitle(response.text)\\n                    else:\\n                        # Try JSON3 format first\\n                        try:\\n                            return self._parse_json3_subtitle(response.text)\\n                        except:\\n                            return self._parse_vtt_subtitle(response.text)\\n                \\n                except Exception as exc:\\n                    logger.warning(\\\"Failed to download subtitle from %s: %s\\\", subtitle_url, exc)\\n                    continue\\n    \\n    raise ValueError(\\\"Could not download subtitle in any supported format\\\")\\n\\ndef _parse_json3_subtitle(self, content: str) -> str:\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Parse YouTube JSON3 subtitle format.\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    import json\\n    data = json.loads(content)\\n    \\n    text_parts = []\\n    if 'events' in data:\\n        for event in data['events']:\\n            if 'segs' in event:\\n                for seg in event['segs']:\\n                    if 'utf8' in seg:\\n                        text_parts.append(seg['utf8'].strip())\\n    \\n    return ' '.join(text_parts)\\n\\ndef _parse_vtt_subtitle(self, content: str) -> str:\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Parse WebVTT subtitle format.\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    import re\\n    \\n    # Remove WEBVTT header and timestamps\\n    lines = content.split('\\\\n')\\n    text_parts = []\\n    \\n    for line in lines:\\n        # Skip headers, timestamps, and empty lines\\n        if line.startswith('WEBVTT') or '-->' in line or line.strip() == '' or re.match(r'^\\\\d', line):\\n            continue\\n        \\n        # Remove HTML tags\\n        text = re.sub(r'<[^>]+>', '', line)\\n        if text.strip():\\n            text_parts.append(text.strip())\\n    \\n    return ' '.join(text_parts)\\n\\ndef _get_language_name(self, lang_code: str) -> str:\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Map language codes to human-readable names.\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    lang_map = {\\n        'en': 'English',\\n        'ru': 'Russian',\\n        'es': 'Spanish',\\n        'fr': 'French',\\n        'de': 'German',\\n        'it': 'Italian',\\n        'pt': 'Portuguese',\\n        'ja': 'Japanese',\\n        'ko': 'Korean',\\n        'zh': 'Chinese',\\n        'ar': 'Arabic',\\n        'hi': 'Hindi',\\n    }\\n    return lang_map.get(lang_code, lang_code.upper())\\n```\\n\\n---\\n\\n## Testing\\n\\nAfter deployment:\\n1. ✅ Verify cookies are obtained through proxy (check logs for \\\"Obtained YouTube cookies via proxy\\\")\\n2. ✅ Verify session IDs rotate (check logs for \\\"Using rotating proxy session ID: X\\\")\\n3. ✅ Test `GET /api/transcripts/list` returns available subtitles\\n4. ✅ Test `POST /api/extract` successfully downloads transcript\\n5. ✅ Verify no \\\"422 Unprocessable Entity\\\" errors\\n6. ✅ Verify no \\\"Sign in to confirm you're not a bot\\\" errors\\n\\n---\\n\\n## Files Modified\\n\\n- `backend/app/services/extractors/youtube.py` — Add cookie-based proxy workaround\\n\\n---\\n\\n## Priority\\n\\n🔴 **Critical** — Current implementation completely broken with proxies.\", \"problem_title\": \"Fix yt-dlp proxy authentication using requests cookie passthrough\", \"repository\": \"DmitriyPolumienko/AI-Content-Reparser\"}",

Pass cookies to `yt-dlp` → bypass IP blocks\\n\\nThis leverages:\\n- ✅ `requests` proven proxy support (already works in the codebase)\\n- ✅ `yt-dlp` powerful YouTube metadata extraction\\n- ✅ Same Webshare rotating proxy infrastructure\\n\\n---\\n\\n## Implementation\\n\\n### **Update `backend/app/services/extractors/youtube.py`**\\n\\n**Add imports:**\\n```python\\nimport requests\\nimport tempfile\\nimport http.cookiejar as cookiejar\\nfrom pathlib import Path\\n```\\n\\n**Add helper method for cookie extraction:**\\n```python\\ndef _get_youtube_cookies_via_proxy(self, video_id: str, proxy_url: str | None) -> str:\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Make a request to YouTube through proxy to get cookies.\\n    Returns path to temporary cookie file for yt-dlp.\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    url = f\\\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v={video_id}\\\"\\n    \\n    try:\\n        session = requests.Session()\\n        \\n        if proxy_url:\\n            session.proxies = {\\n                'http': proxy_url,\\n                'https': proxy_url,\\n            }\\n        \\n        # Make request to get cookies\\n        response = session.get(\\n            url,\\n            headers={\\n                'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/120.0.0.0 Safari/537.36',\\n                'Accept': 'text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,*/*;q=0.8',\\n                'Accept-Language': 'en-US,en;q=0.9',\\n            },\\n            timeout=15,\\n        )\\n        response.raise_for_status()\\n        \\n        # Save cookies to temp file in Netscape format for yt-dlp\\n        cookie_file = tempfile.NamedTemporaryFile(mode='w', suffix='.txt', delete=False)\\n        \\n        # Write Netscape cookie file header\\n        cookie_file.write(\\\"# Netscape HTTP Cookie File\\\\n\\\")\\n        cookie_file.write(\\\"# This is a generated file! Do not edit.\\\\n\\\\n\\\")\\n        \\n        # Convert requests cookies to Netscape format\\n        for cookie in session.cookies:\\n            cookie_file.write(\\n                f\\\"{cookie.domain}\\\\t\\\"\\n                f\\\"{'TRUE' if cookie.domain.startswith('.') else 'FALSE'}\\\\t\\\"\\n                f\\\"{cookie.path}\\\\t\\\"\\n                f\\\"{'TRUE' if cookie.secure else 'FALSE'}\\\\t\\\"\\n                f\\\"{cookie.expires if cookie.expires else 0}\\\\t\\\"\\n                f\\\"{cookie.name}\\\\t\\\"\\n                f\\\"{cookie.value}\\\\n\\\"\\n            )\\n        \\n        cookie_file.close()\\n        logger.info(\\\"Obtained YouTube cookies via proxy, saved to %s\\\", cookie_file.name)\\n        return cookie_file.name\\n    \\n    except Exception as exc:\\n        logger.warning(\\\"Failed to get cookies via proxy: %s\\\", exc)\\n        raise\\n```\\n\\n**Update `list_transcripts()` method:**\\n```python\\ndef list_transcripts(self, url: str) -> list:\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    List available transcripts for a YouTube video without downloading them.\\n    \\n    Returns a list of dicts with keys: language_code, language_name, is_generated, is_translatable.\\n    Manual transcripts are listed before auto-generated ones.\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    video_id = self._extract_video_id(url)\\n    \\n    proxy_active = self._rotating_proxy_configured() or bool(self._legacy_proxy_list)\\n    max_attempts = self.MAX_PROXY_RETRIES if proxy_active else 1\\n    last_exception: Exception | None = None\\n    \\n    for attempt in range(max_attempts):\\n        cookie_file_path = None\\n        try:\\n            # Get cookies through proxy if configured\\n            proxy_url = None\\n            if self._rotating_proxy_configured():\\n                proxy_url = self._get_random_proxy()\\n            elif self._legacy_proxy_list:\\n                proxy_url = random.choice(self._legacy_proxy_list)\\n                logger.info(\\\"Using static proxy from list\\\")\\n            \\n            if proxy_url:\\n                cookie_file_path = self._get_youtube_cookies_via_proxy(video_id, proxy_url)\\n            \\n            # Configure yt-dlp with cookies (no direct proxy)\\n            ydl_opts = {\\n                'skip_download': True,\\n                'quiet': True,\\n                'no_warnings': True,\\n                'extract_flat': False,\\n            }\\n            \\n            if cookie_file_path:\\n                ydl_opts['cookiefile'] = cookie_file_path\\n            \\n            with yt_dlp.YoutubeDL(ydl_opts) as ydl:\\n                info = ydl.extract_info(f'https://youtube.com/watch?v={video_id}', download=False)\\n                \\n                if not info:\\n                    raise ValueError(\\\"Could not extract video information\\\")\\n                \\n                subtitles = info.get('subtitles', {})\\n                automatic_captions = info.get('automatic_captions', {})\\n                \\n                available = []\\n                \\n                # Manual subtitles first\\n                for lang_code in subtitles.keys():\\n                    available.append({\\n                        \\\"language_code\\\": lang_code,\\n                        \\\"language_name\\\": self._get_language_name(lang_code),\\n                        \\\"is_generated\\\": False,\\n                        \\\"is_translatable\\\": False,\\n                    })\\n                \\n                # Auto-generated subtitles second (only if not already in manual)\\n                for lang_code in automatic_captions.keys():\\n                    if lang_code not in subtitles:\\n                        available.append({\\n                            \\\"language_code\\\": lang_code,\\n                            \\\"language_name\\\": f\\\"{self._get_language_name(lang_code)} (auto-generated)\\\",\\n                            \\\"is_generated\\\": True,\\n                            \\\"is_translatable\\\": False,\\n                        })\\n                \\n                logger.info(\\\"Listed %d transcripts for %s\\\", len(available), video_id)\\n                return available\\n        \\n        except Exception as exc:\\n            last_exception = exc\\n            logger.warning(\\\"List attempt %d failed: %s\\\", attempt + 1, exc)\\n        \\n        finally:\\n            # Clean up temp cookie file\\n            if cookie_file_path and Path(cookie_file_path).exists():\\n                try:\\n                    Path(cookie_file_path).unlink()\\n                except Exception as cleanup_exc:\\n                    logger.warning(\\\"Failed to delete temp cookie file: %s\\\", cleanup_exc)\\n    \\n    error_msg = f\\\"Failed to list transcripts after {max_attempts} attempt(s).\\\"\\n    if proxy_active:\\n        error_msg += \\\" All proxies failed. YouTube may be blocking these IPs.\\\"\\n    else:\\n        error_msg += \\\" No proxies configured. YouTube is likely blocking your server IP.\\\"\\n    \\n    raise RuntimeError(f\\\"{error_msg} Last error: {last_exception}\\\") from last_exception\\n```\\n\\n**Update `extract_transcript()` method:**\\n```python\\ndef extract_transcript(\\n    self,\\n    url: str,\\n    language: str | None = None,\\n    prefer_manual: bool = True,\\n) -> str:\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Extract transcript from YouTube video.\\n    Uses proxy rotation with retry logic if proxies are configured.\\n    \\n    Args:\\n        url: YouTube video URL.\\n        language: YouTube language code (e.g. \\\"en\\\", \\\"ru\\\"). If None, falls back to\\n                  [\\\"en\\\", \\\"ru\\\"] in order of preference.\\n        prefer_manual: When True, prefer manual transcripts over auto-generated ones.\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    video_id = self._extract_video_id(url)\\n    \\n    proxy_active = self._rotating_proxy_configured() or bool(self._legacy_proxy_list)\\n    max_attempts = self.MAX_PROXY_RETRIES if proxy_active else 1\\n    last_exception: Exception | None = None\\n    \\n    for attempt in range(max_attempts):\\n        cookie_file_path = None\\n        try:\\n            # Get cookies through proxy if configured\\n            proxy_url = None\\n            if self._rotating_proxy_configured():\\n                proxy_url = self._get_random_proxy()\\n            elif self._legacy_proxy_list:\\n                proxy_url = random.choice(self._legacy_proxy_list)\\n                logger.info(\\\"Using static proxy from list\\\")\\n            \\n            if proxy_url:\\n                cookie_file_path = self._get_youtube_cookies_via_proxy(video_id, proxy_url)\\n            \\n            # Configure yt-dlp with cookies\\n            ydl_opts = {\\n                'skip_download': True,\\n                'writesubtitles': True,\\n                'writeautomaticsub': True,\\n                'quiet': True,\\n                'no_warnings': True,\\n            }\\n            \\n            if cookie_file_path:\\n                ydl_opts['cookiefile'] = cookie_file_path\\n            \\n            with yt_dlp.YoutubeDL(ydl_opts) as ydl:\\n                info = ydl.extract_info(f'https://youtube.com/watch?v={video_id}', download=False)\\n                \\n                if not info:\\n                    raise ValueError(\\\"Could not extract video information\\\")\\n                \\n                subtitles = info.get('subtitles', {})\\n                automatic_captions = info.get('automatic_captions', {})\\n                \\n                lang_candidates = [language] if language else ['en', 'ru']\\n                \\n                # Find best matching subtitle\\n                for lang in lang_candidates:\\n                    if prefer_manual and lang in subtitles:\\n                        text = self._download_and_parse_subtitle(subtitles[lang], proxy_url)\\n                        logger.info(\\\"Successfully extracted manual transcript for %s (attempt %d)\\\", video_id, attempt + 1)\\n                        return text\\n                    elif lang in automatic_captions:\\n                        text = self._download_and_parse_subtitle(automatic_captions[lang], proxy_url)\\n                        logger.info(\\\"Successfully extracted auto-generated transcript for %s (attempt %d)\\\", video_id, attempt + 1)\\n                        return text\\n                \\n                # Fallback: try opposite preference\\n                for lang in lang_candidates:\\n                    if not prefer_manual and lang in subtitles:\\n                        text = self._download_and_parse_subtitle(subtitles[lang], proxy_url)\\n                        logger.info(\\\"Successfully extracted manual transcript for %s (attempt %d)\\\", video_id, attempt + 1)\\n                        return text\\n                \\n                raise ValueError(f\\\"No transcript found for language(s): {', '.join(lang_candidates)}\\\")\\n        \\n        except ValueError:\\n            # Don't retry on \\\"no transcript found\\\" errors\\n            raise\\n        \\n        except Exception as exc:\\n            last_exception = exc\\n            logger.warning(\\\"Attempt %d failed: %s\\\", attempt + 1, exc)\\n        \\n        finally:\\n            # Clean up temp cookie file\\n            if cookie_file_path and Path(cookie_file_path).exists():\\n                try:\\n                    Path(cookie_file_path).unlink()\\n                except Exception as cleanup_exc:\\n                    logger.warning(\\\"Failed to delete temp cookie file: %s\\\", cleanup_exc)\\n    \\n    error_msg = f\\\"Failed to extract transcript after {max_attempts} attempt(s).\\\"\\n    if proxy_active:\\n        error_msg += \\\" All proxies failed. YouTube may be blocking these IPs.\\\"\\n    else:\\n        error_msg += \\\" No proxies configured. YouTube is likely blocking your server IP.\\\"\\n    \\n    raise RuntimeError(f\\\"{error_msg} Last error: {last_exception}\\\") from last_exception\\n```\\n\\n**Add subtitle download helper:**\\n```python\\ndef _download_and_parse_subtitle(self, formats: list, proxy_url: str | None) -> str:\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Download and parse subtitle from the first available format.\\n    Uses proxy if provided.\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    for fmt in formats:\\n        if fmt.get('ext') in ['json3', 'srv3', 'vtt', 'srv1', 'srv2']:\\n            subtitle_url = fmt.get('url')\\n            if subtitle_url:\\n                try:\\n                    session = requests.Session()\\n                    if proxy_url:\\n                        session.proxies = {'http': proxy_url, 'https': proxy_url}\\n                    \\n                    response = session.get(subtitle_url, timeout=15)\\n                    response.raise_for_status()\\n                    \\n                    # Parse based on format\\n                    if fmt.get('ext') == 'json3':\\n                        return self._parse_json3_subtitle(response.text)\\n                    elif fmt.get('ext') == 'vtt':\\n                        return self._parse_vtt_subtitle(response.text)\\n                    else:\\n                        # Try JSON3 format first\\n                        try:\\n                            return self._parse_json3_subtitle(response.text)\\n                        except:\\n                            return self._parse_vtt_subtitle(response.text)\\n                \\n                except Exception as exc:\\n                    logger.warning(\\\"Failed to download subtitle from %s: %s\\\", subtitle_url, exc)\\n                    continue\\n    \\n    raise ValueError(\\\"Could not download subtitle in any supported format\\\")\\n\\ndef _parse_json3_subtitle(self, content: str) -> str:\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Parse YouTube JSON3 subtitle format.\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    import json\\n    data = json.loads(content)\\n    \\n    text_parts = []\\n    if 'events' in data:\\n        for event in data['events']:\\n            if 'segs' in event:\\n                for seg in event['segs']:\\n                    if 'utf8' in seg:\\n                        text_parts.append(seg['utf8'].strip())\\n    \\n    return ' '.join(text_parts)\\n\\ndef _parse_vtt_subtitle(self, content: str) -> str:\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Parse WebVTT subtitle format.\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    import re\\n    \\n    # Remove WEBVTT header and timestamps\\n    lines = content.split('\\\\n')\\n    text_parts = []\\n    \\n    for line in lines:\\n        # Skip headers, timestamps, and empty lines\\n        if line.startswith('WEBVTT') or '-->' in line or line.strip() == '' or re.match(r'^\\\\d', line):\\n            continue\\n        \\n        # Remove HTML tags\\n        text = re.sub(r'<[^>]+>', '', line)\\n        if text.strip():\\n            text_parts.append(text.strip())\\n    \\n    return ' '.join(text_parts)\\n\\ndef _get_language_name(self, lang_code: str) -> str:\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Map language codes to human-readable names.\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    lang_map = {\\n        'en': 'English',\\n        'ru': 'Russian',\\n        'es': 'Spanish',\\n        'fr': 'French',\\n        'de': 'German',\\n        'it': 'Italian',\\n        'pt': 'Portuguese',\\n        'ja': 'Japanese',\\n        'ko': 'Korean',\\n        'zh': 'Chinese',\\n        'ar': 'Arabic',\\n        'hi': 'Hindi',\\n    }\\n    return lang_map.get(lang_code, lang_code.upper())\\n```\\n\\n---\\n\\n## Testing\\n\\nAfter deployment:\\n1. ✅ Verify cookies are obtained through proxy (check logs for \\\"Obtained YouTube cookies via proxy\\\")\\n2. ✅ Verify session IDs rotate (check logs for \\\"Using rotating proxy session ID: X\\\")\\n3. ✅ Test `GET /api/transcripts/list` returns available subtitles\\n4. ✅ Test `POST /api/extract` successfully downloads transcript\\n5. ✅ Verify no \\\"422 Unprocessable Entity\\\" errors\\n6. ✅ Verify no \\\"Sign in to confirm you're not a bot\\\" errors\\n\\n---\\n\\n## Files Modified\\n\\n- `backend/app/services/extractors/youtube.py` — Add cookie-based proxy workaround\\n\\n---\\n\\n## Priority\\n\\n🔴 **Critical** — Current implementation completely broken with proxies.\", \"problem_title\": \"Fix yt-dlp proxy authentication using requests cookie passthrough\", \"repository\": \"DmitriyPolumienko/AI-Content-Reparser\"}",
